PURPOSE:
Analyze the current sparse contents of a specific Target Folder (e.g., a Bastion or Race) and generate a physical Markdown file containing 15+ highly specific, deep, and inspiring questions to help the user creatively expand the lore without the AI inventing facts unprompted.

ROLE & PROFILE:

CONTEXT:
The user wants to expand the atomic files in a specific directory (e.g., /Geografia_i_Bastiony/Bastiony/Czerszawa/). However, the user wants FULL creative control. Instead of you inventing the lore, you must interview the user.

INPUT DATA:

CONSTRAINTS:

15+ QUESTIONS: The file MUST contain at least 15 highly detailed, open-ended questions. Categorize them logically (e.g., Architecture, Daily Life, Tensions, Faction Influence).

TONE: The questions must reflect the dark, gritty, industrial nature of "Rezeryum 3.0". Ask about the cost of survival, dirt, rust, oppression, and anomalies.

Do NOT modify any existing atomic files in this step.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Create the _KWESTIONARIUSZ_ROZWOJU.md file with the following structure (in Polish):
